-- Provera
SELECT
  k."TakmicenjeId",
  COUNT(*) AS broj_utakmica
FROM "Utakmica" u
JOIN "Kolo" k ON k."Id" = u."KoloId"
GROUP BY k."TakmicenjeId"
ORDER BY k."TakmicenjeId";


ALTER TABLE "Utakmica"
ALTER COLUMN "DatumPocetkaUtakmice" DROP DEFAULT;
ALTER TABLE "Utakmica"
ADD COLUMN "DatumPocetkaUtakmice_ts" TIMESTAMP;
UPDATE "Utakmica"
SET "DatumPocetkaUtakmice_ts" =
  CASE
    -- ISO: 2025-11-01 17:00:00 (ili sa T)
    WHEN "DatumPocetkaUtakmice" ~ '^\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2}'
      THEN ("DatumPocetkaUtakmice")::timestamp

    -- DD.MM.YYYY (bez vremena) -> dodaj 18:00
    WHEN "DatumPocetkaUtakmice" ~ '^\d{2}\.\d{2}\.\d{4}$'
      THEN to_timestamp("DatumPocetkaUtakmice" || ' 18:00', 'DD.MM.YYYY HH24:MI')::timestamp

    -- DD.MM.YYYY HH:MI
    WHEN "DatumPocetkaUtakmice" ~ '^\d{2}\.\d{2}\.\d{4} \d{2}:\d{2}$'
      THEN to_timestamp("DatumPocetkaUtakmice", 'DD.MM.YYYY HH24:MI')::timestamp

    -- DD.MM.YYYY HH:MI:SS
    WHEN "DatumPocetkaUtakmice" ~ '^\d{2}\.\d{2}\.\d{4} \d{2}:\d{2}:\d{2}$'
      THEN to_timestamp("DatumPocetkaUtakmice", 'DD.MM.YYYY HH24:MI:SS')::timestamp

    ELSE NULL
  END;


SELECT "Id", "DatumPocetkaUtakmice"
FROM "Utakmica"
WHERE "DatumPocetkaUtakmice_ts" IS NULL
  AND "DatumPocetkaUtakmice" IS NOT NULL
LIMIT 50;
ALTER TABLE "Utakmica" DROP COLUMN "DatumPocetkaUtakmice";
ALTER TABLE "Utakmica" RENAME COLUMN "DatumPocetkaUtakmice_ts" TO "DatumPocetkaUtakmice";
--DODAVANJE UTAKMICA SA STATISTIKOM ZA EUROLEAGUE
BEGIN;

DO $$
DECLARE
  v_takmicenje_id int := 9;  -- <<< PROMENI NA 9
  v_base_ut int;
  v_base_st int;
BEGIN

  -- (0) Privremeno dozvoli NULL (zbog ciklične veze)
  ALTER TABLE "Utakmica" ALTER COLUMN "StatistikaId" DROP NOT NULL;

  -- (1) OBRIŠI samo utakmice/statistike za ovo takmičenje
  DELETE FROM "Statistika" s
  USING "Utakmica" u, "Kolo" k
  WHERE s."UtakmicaId" = u."Id"
    AND u."KoloId" = k."Id"
    AND k."TakmicenjeId" = v_takmicenje_id;

  DELETE FROM "Utakmica" u
  USING "Kolo" k
  WHERE u."KoloId" = k."Id"
    AND k."TakmicenjeId" = v_takmicenje_id;

  -- (2) OFFSET da nema sudara PK
  SELECT COALESCE(MAX("Id"), 0) INTO v_base_ut FROM "Utakmica";
  SELECT COALESCE(MAX("Id"), 0) INTO v_base_st FROM "Statistika";

  -- (3) tmp_schedule: round-robin + revanši (svako 2x)
  DROP TABLE IF EXISTS tmp_schedule;
  CREATE TEMP TABLE tmp_schedule AS
  WITH RECURSIVE
  teams AS (
    SELECT
      t."KlubId" AS klub_id,
      ROW_NUMBER() OVER (ORDER BY t."KlubId") AS rn
    FROM "Tabela" t
    WHERE t."TakmicenjeId" = v_takmicenje_id
  ),
  init AS (
    SELECT
      array_agg(klub_id ORDER BY rn) AS arr,
      COUNT(*)::int AS n
    FROM teams
  ),
  rounds AS (
    SELECT 1 AS r, arr, n
    FROM init
    UNION ALL
    SELECT
      r + 1,
      (arr[1:1] || arr[n:n] || arr[2:n-1])::int[],
      n
    FROM rounds
    WHERE r < (SELECT n - 1 FROM init)
  ),
  pairs_first_leg AS (
    SELECT
      r,
      i,
      CASE WHEN (r + i) % 2 = 0 THEN arr[i] ELSE arr[n+1-i] END AS home_id,
      CASE WHEN (r + i) % 2 = 0 THEN arr[n+1-i] ELSE arr[i] END AS away_id
    FROM rounds
    CROSS JOIN LATERAL generate_series(1, (SELECT n/2 FROM init)) AS i
  ),
  pairs_all AS (
    SELECT r, home_id, away_id FROM pairs_first_leg
    UNION ALL
    SELECT r + (SELECT n - 1 FROM init) AS r, away_id AS home_id, home_id AS away_id
    FROM pairs_first_leg
  ),
  pair_names AS (
    SELECT
      p.r,
      kh."Naziv" AS domacin,
      kg."Naziv" AS gost
    FROM pairs_all p
    JOIN "Klub" kh ON kh."Id" = p.home_id
    JOIN "Klub" kg ON kg."Id" = p.away_id
  ),
  kolodata AS (
    -- očekuje se da imaš bar (n-1)*2 kola za ovo takmičenje
    SELECT
      k."Id" AS kolo_id,
      k."BrojKola" AS r,
      k."PocetakKola"::timestamp AS datum_ts
    FROM "Kolo" k
    WHERE k."TakmicenjeId" = v_takmicenje_id
      AND k."TipKola" = 1
  )
  SELECT
    (v_base_ut + row_number() OVER (ORDER BY pn.r, pn.domacin, pn.gost)) AS utakmica_id,
    (v_base_st + row_number() OVER (ORDER BY pn.r, pn.domacin, pn.gost)) AS statistika_id,
    pn.domacin,
    pn.gost,
    kd.kolo_id,
    kd.datum_ts
  FROM pair_names pn
  JOIN kolodata kd ON kd.r = pn.r;

  -- (4) UBACI UTAKMICE (Uzivo zavisi od datuma)
  INSERT INTO "Utakmica"
  (
    "Id","Uzivo","Domacin","Gost","Lokacija","Rezultat","KoloId","StatistikaId","DatumPocetkaUtakmice"
  )
  SELECT
    s.utakmica_id,
    CASE WHEN s.datum_ts::date = CURRENT_DATE THEN TRUE ELSE FALSE END,
    s.domacin,
    s.gost,
    'Hala ' || s.domacin,
    '0:0',
    s.kolo_id,
    NULL,
    s.datum_ts
  FROM tmp_schedule s
  ORDER BY s.utakmica_id;

  -- (5) UBACI STATISTIKE: SAMO KOŠARKA POLJA (ostalo ostaje NULL)
  INSERT INTO "Statistika"
  (
    "Id",
    "TrenutniMinut",
    "UtakmicaId",
    "Sport",

    "PrvaCetDomacin","PrvaCetGost",
    "DrugaCetDomacin","DrugaCetGost",
    "TrecaCetDomacin","TrecaCetGost",
    "CetvCetDomacin","CetvCetGost",

    "TwoPointDomacin","TwoPointGost",
    "ThreePointDomacin","ThreePointGost",
    "FreeThrowDomacin","FreeThrowGost",

    "ReboundsDomacin","ReboundsGost",
    "StealsDomacin","StealsGost",
    "BlocksDomacin","BlocksGost"
  )
  SELECT
    s.statistika_id,

    CASE
      WHEN s.datum_ts::date < CURRENT_DATE THEN 40
      WHEN s.datum_ts::date > CURRENT_DATE THEN 0
      ELSE live_meta.minut
    END,

    s.utakmica_id,
    2,

    -- Q1
    CASE WHEN s.datum_ts::date > CURRENT_DATE THEN 0
         WHEN s.datum_ts::date < CURRENT_DATE THEN full_h.q1
         ELSE live.q1_h END,
    CASE WHEN s.datum_ts::date > CURRENT_DATE THEN 0
         WHEN s.datum_ts::date < CURRENT_DATE THEN full_a.q1
         ELSE live.q1_a END,

    -- Q2
    CASE WHEN s.datum_ts::date > CURRENT_DATE THEN 0
         WHEN s.datum_ts::date < CURRENT_DATE THEN full_h.q2
         ELSE live.q2_h END,
    CASE WHEN s.datum_ts::date > CURRENT_DATE THEN 0
         WHEN s.datum_ts::date < CURRENT_DATE THEN full_a.q2
         ELSE live.q2_a END,

    -- Q3
    CASE WHEN s.datum_ts::date > CURRENT_DATE THEN 0
         WHEN s.datum_ts::date < CURRENT_DATE THEN full_h.q3
         ELSE live.q3_h END,
    CASE WHEN s.datum_ts::date > CURRENT_DATE THEN 0
         WHEN s.datum_ts::date < CURRENT_DATE THEN full_a.q3
         ELSE live.q3_a END,

    -- Q4
    CASE WHEN s.datum_ts::date > CURRENT_DATE THEN 0
         WHEN s.datum_ts::date < CURRENT_DATE THEN full_h.q4
         ELSE live.q4_h END,
    CASE WHEN s.datum_ts::date > CURRENT_DATE THEN 0
         WHEN s.datum_ts::date < CURRENT_DATE THEN full_a.q4
         ELSE live.q4_a END,

    -- pogodjeni šutevi
    CASE WHEN s.datum_ts::date > CURRENT_DATE THEN 0
         WHEN s.datum_ts::date < CURRENT_DATE THEN shots.tp_h
         ELSE live.tp_h END,
    CASE WHEN s.datum_ts::date > CURRENT_DATE THEN 0
         WHEN s.datum_ts::date < CURRENT_DATE THEN shots.tp_a
         ELSE live.tp_a END,

    CASE WHEN s.datum_ts::date > CURRENT_DATE THEN 0
         WHEN s.datum_ts::date < CURRENT_DATE THEN shots.t3_h
         ELSE live.t3_h END,
    CASE WHEN s.datum_ts::date > CURRENT_DATE THEN 0
         WHEN s.datum_ts::date < CURRENT_DATE THEN shots.t3_a
         ELSE live.t3_a END,

    CASE WHEN s.datum_ts::date > CURRENT_DATE THEN 0
         WHEN s.datum_ts::date < CURRENT_DATE THEN shots.ft_h
         ELSE live.ft_h END,
    CASE WHEN s.datum_ts::date > CURRENT_DATE THEN 0
         WHEN s.datum_ts::date < CURRENT_DATE THEN shots.ft_a
         ELSE live.ft_a END,

    -- rebounds/steals/blocks
    CASE WHEN s.datum_ts::date > CURRENT_DATE THEN 0
         WHEN s.datum_ts::date < CURRENT_DATE THEN (28 + (s.utakmica_id % 18))
         ELSE live.reb_h END,
    CASE WHEN s.datum_ts::date > CURRENT_DATE THEN 0
         WHEN s.datum_ts::date < CURRENT_DATE THEN (28 + ((s.utakmica_id+5) % 18))
         ELSE live.reb_a END,

    CASE WHEN s.datum_ts::date > CURRENT_DATE THEN 0
         WHEN s.datum_ts::date < CURRENT_DATE THEN (4 + (s.utakmica_id % 11))
         ELSE live.stl_h END,
    CASE WHEN s.datum_ts::date > CURRENT_DATE THEN 0
         WHEN s.datum_ts::date < CURRENT_DATE THEN (4 + ((s.utakmica_id+2) % 11))
         ELSE live.stl_a END,

    CASE WHEN s.datum_ts::date > CURRENT_DATE THEN 0
         WHEN s.datum_ts::date < CURRENT_DATE THEN (1 + (s.utakmica_id % 8))
         ELSE live.blk_h END,
    CASE WHEN s.datum_ts::date > CURRENT_DATE THEN 0
         WHEN s.datum_ts::date < CURRENT_DATE THEN (1 + ((s.utakmica_id+4) % 8))
         ELSE live.blk_a END

  FROM tmp_schedule s

  -- full-game šutevi + total
  CROSS JOIN LATERAL (
    SELECT
      (18 + (s.utakmica_id % 13))                  AS tp_h,
      (18 + ((s.utakmica_id+3) % 13))              AS tp_a,
      (6  + (s.utakmica_id % 10))                  AS t3_h,
      (6  + ((s.utakmica_id+3) % 10))              AS t3_a,
      (10 + (s.utakmica_id % 16))                  AS ft_h,
      (10 + ((s.utakmica_id+3) % 16))              AS ft_a,
      (2*(18 + (s.utakmica_id % 13)) + 3*(6 + (s.utakmica_id % 10)) + (10 + (s.utakmica_id % 16)))              AS total_h,
      (2*(18 + ((s.utakmica_id+3) % 13)) + 3*(6 + ((s.utakmica_id+3) % 10)) + (10 + ((s.utakmica_id+3) % 16)))  AS total_a
  ) shots

  -- full četvrtine domaćin
  CROSS JOIN LATERAL (
    SELECT q1_adj AS q1, q2 AS q2, q3 AS q3, (q4_raw + adj) AS q4
    FROM (
      SELECT (shots.total_h / 4)::int AS base, (10 + (s.utakmica_id % 9))::int AS delta
    ) b
    CROSS JOIN LATERAL (
      SELECT
        LEAST(shots.total_h - 18, b.base + b.delta) AS q1_raw,
        GREATEST(6, b.base - b.delta)               AS q2,
        GREATEST(6, b.base - (b.delta/2))           AS q3
    ) x
    CROSS JOIN LATERAL (
      SELECT (shots.total_h - (x.q1_raw + x.q2 + x.q3)) AS q4_raw
    ) y
    CROSS JOIN LATERAL (
      SELECT GREATEST(0, 6 - y.q4_raw) AS adj,
             (x.q1_raw - GREATEST(0, 6 - y.q4_raw)) AS q1_adj
    ) z
  ) full_h

  -- full četvrtine gost
  CROSS JOIN LATERAL (
    SELECT q1_adj AS q1, q2 AS q2, q3_adj AS q3, (q4_raw + adj) AS q4
    FROM (
      SELECT (shots.total_a / 4)::int AS base, (9 + ((s.utakmica_id+4) % 10))::int AS delta
    ) b
    CROSS JOIN LATERAL (
      SELECT
        LEAST(shots.total_a - 18, b.base + (b.delta/2)) AS q1_raw,
        GREATEST(6, b.base - (b.delta/2))               AS q2,
        LEAST(shots.total_a - 18, b.base + b.delta)     AS q3_raw
    ) x
    CROSS JOIN LATERAL (
      SELECT (shots.total_a - (x.q1_raw + x.q2 + x.q3_raw)) AS q4_raw
    ) y
    CROSS JOIN LATERAL (
      SELECT GREATEST(0, 6 - y.q4_raw) AS adj,
             (x.q3_raw - GREATEST(0, 6 - y.q4_raw)) AS q3_adj,
             x.q1_raw AS q1_adj
    ) z
  ) full_a

  -- LIVE meta (samo za danas)
  CROSS JOIN LATERAL (
    SELECT
      ((s.utakmica_id % 4) + 1)::int AS q_active,
      (0.35 + ((s.utakmica_id % 6) * 0.1))::numeric AS prog,
      CASE ((s.utakmica_id % 4) + 1)
        WHEN 1 THEN 5  + (s.utakmica_id % 6)
        WHEN 2 THEN 15 + (s.utakmica_id % 6)
        WHEN 3 THEN 25 + (s.utakmica_id % 6)
        ELSE        35 + (s.utakmica_id % 6)
      END AS minut,
      ( (((s.utakmica_id % 4) + 1) - 1) + (0.35 + ((s.utakmica_id % 6) * 0.1)) ) / 4.0 AS game_ratio
  ) live_meta

  -- LIVE vrednosti (četvrtine + skalirani boxscore)
  CROSS JOIN LATERAL (
    SELECT
      CASE WHEN s.datum_ts::date <> CURRENT_DATE THEN full_h.q1
           WHEN live_meta.q_active > 1 THEN full_h.q1
           ELSE GREATEST(0, (full_h.q1 * live_meta.prog)::int) END AS q1_h,
      CASE WHEN s.datum_ts::date <> CURRENT_DATE THEN full_a.q1
           WHEN live_meta.q_active > 1 THEN full_a.q1
           ELSE GREATEST(0, (full_a.q1 * live_meta.prog)::int) END AS q1_a,

      CASE WHEN s.datum_ts::date <> CURRENT_DATE THEN full_h.q2
           WHEN live_meta.q_active > 2 THEN full_h.q2
           WHEN live_meta.q_active = 2 THEN GREATEST(0, (full_h.q2 * live_meta.prog)::int)
           ELSE 0 END AS q2_h,
      CASE WHEN s.datum_ts::date <> CURRENT_DATE THEN full_a.q2
           WHEN live_meta.q_active > 2 THEN full_a.q2
           WHEN live_meta.q_active = 2 THEN GREATEST(0, (full_a.q2 * live_meta.prog)::int)
           ELSE 0 END AS q2_a,

      CASE WHEN s.datum_ts::date <> CURRENT_DATE THEN full_h.q3
           WHEN live_meta.q_active > 3 THEN full_h.q3
           WHEN live_meta.q_active = 3 THEN GREATEST(0, (full_h.q3 * live_meta.prog)::int)
           ELSE 0 END AS q3_h,
      CASE WHEN s.datum_ts::date <> CURRENT_DATE THEN full_a.q3
           WHEN live_meta.q_active > 3 THEN full_a.q3
           WHEN live_meta.q_active = 3 THEN GREATEST(0, (full_a.q3 * live_meta.prog)::int)
           ELSE 0 END AS q3_a,

      CASE WHEN s.datum_ts::date <> CURRENT_DATE THEN full_h.q4
           WHEN live_meta.q_active = 4 THEN GREATEST(0, (full_h.q4 * live_meta.prog)::int)
           ELSE 0 END AS q4_h,
      CASE WHEN s.datum_ts::date <> CURRENT_DATE THEN full_a.q4
           WHEN live_meta.q_active = 4 THEN GREATEST(0, (full_a.q4 * live_meta.prog)::int)
           ELSE 0 END AS q4_a,

      GREATEST(0, (shots.tp_h * live_meta.game_ratio)::int) AS tp_h,
      GREATEST(0, (shots.tp_a * live_meta.game_ratio)::int) AS tp_a,
      GREATEST(0, (shots.t3_h * live_meta.game_ratio)::int) AS t3_h,
      GREATEST(0, (shots.t3_a * live_meta.game_ratio)::int) AS t3_a,
      GREATEST(0, (shots.ft_h * live_meta.game_ratio)::int) AS ft_h,
      GREATEST(0, (shots.ft_a * live_meta.game_ratio)::int) AS ft_a,

      GREATEST(0, ((28 + (s.utakmica_id % 18)) * live_meta.game_ratio)::int) AS reb_h,
      GREATEST(0, ((28 + ((s.utakmica_id+5) % 18)) * live_meta.game_ratio)::int) AS reb_a,
      GREATEST(0, ((4 + (s.utakmica_id % 11)) * live_meta.game_ratio)::int) AS stl_h,
      GREATEST(0, ((4 + ((s.utakmica_id+2) % 11)) * live_meta.game_ratio)::int) AS stl_a,
      GREATEST(0, ((1 + (s.utakmica_id % 8)) * live_meta.game_ratio)::int) AS blk_h,
      GREATEST(0, ((1 + ((s.utakmica_id+4) % 8)) * live_meta.game_ratio)::int) AS blk_a
  ) live
  ORDER BY s.statistika_id;

  -- (6) VEŽI utakmice -> statistike (kao tvoja skripta)
  UPDATE "Utakmica" u
  SET "StatistikaId" = s.statistika_id
  FROM tmp_schedule s
  WHERE u."Id" = s.utakmica_id;

  -- (7) UPDATE Rezultat samo za ove utakmice (format DOMACIN:GOST)
  UPDATE "Utakmica" u
  SET "Rezultat" =
    (COALESCE(st."PrvaCetDomacin",0) + COALESCE(st."DrugaCetDomacin",0) +
     COALESCE(st."TrecaCetDomacin",0) + COALESCE(st."CetvCetDomacin",0))::text
    || ':' ||
    (COALESCE(st."PrvaCetGost",0) + COALESCE(st."DrugaCetGost",0) +
     COALESCE(st."TrecaCetGost",0) + COALESCE(st."CetvCetGost",0))::text
  FROM "Statistika" st, tmp_schedule s
  WHERE u."Id" = s.utakmica_id
    AND st."Id" = s.statistika_id;

  -- (8) Vrati NOT NULL
  ALTER TABLE "Utakmica" ALTER COLUMN "StatistikaId" SET NOT NULL;

END $$;

COMMIT;
ALTER TABLE "Statistika"
ADD COLUMN "AsistencijeDomacin" INT,
ADD COLUMN "AsistencijeGost" INT;
UPDATE "Statistika" s
SET
  "AsistencijeDomacin" = CASE
    WHEN s."Sport" = 1 THEN (random() * 6)::int          -- fudbal 0-5
    WHEN s."Sport" = 2 THEN ((random() * 21)::int + 10)  -- kosarka 10-30
    WHEN s."Sport" = 3 THEN ((random() * 8)::int + 3)    -- vaterpolo 3-10
    ELSE NULL
  END,
  "AsistencijeGost" = CASE
    WHEN s."Sport" = 1 THEN (random() * 6)::int
    WHEN s."Sport" = 2 THEN ((random() * 21)::int + 10)
    WHEN s."Sport" = 3 THEN ((random() * 8)::int + 3)
    ELSE NULL
  END
FROM "Utakmica" u
WHERE u."Id" = s."UtakmicaId"
  AND u."DatumPocetkaUtakmice" < (now()::date);   -- “pre danas”

--DODAVANJE UTAKMICA ZA EUROCUP

BEGIN;

DO $$
DECLARE
  v_takmicenje_id int := 10;
  v_base_ut int;
  v_base_st int;
BEGIN
  -- 0) Privremeno dozvoli NULL (zbog ciklične veze)
  ALTER TABLE "Utakmica" ALTER COLUMN "StatistikaId" DROP NOT NULL;

  -- 1) OBRIŠI postojeće utakmice/statistike za ovo takmičenje
  DELETE FROM "Statistika" s
  USING "Utakmica" u, "Kolo" k
  WHERE s."UtakmicaId" = u."Id"
    AND u."KoloId" = k."Id"
    AND k."TakmicenjeId" = v_takmicenje_id;

  DELETE FROM "Utakmica" u
  USING "Kolo" k
  WHERE u."KoloId" = k."Id"
    AND k."TakmicenjeId" = v_takmicenje_id;

  -- 2) OFFSETI
  SELECT COALESCE(MAX("Id"), 0) INTO v_base_ut FROM "Utakmica";
  SELECT COALESCE(MAX("Id"), 0) INTO v_base_st FROM "Statistika";

  DROP TABLE IF EXISTS tmp_schedule;

  -- 3) RASPORED PO GRUPAMA (round-robin) + REVANŠI
  CREATE TEMP TABLE tmp_schedule AS
  WITH RECURSIVE
  teams AS (
    SELECT
      t."NazivTabele" AS grp,
      t."KlubId"     AS klub_id,
      ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY t."NazivTabele" ORDER BY t."KlubId") AS rn
    FROM "Tabela" t
    WHERE t."TakmicenjeId" = v_takmicenje_id
      AND t."NazivTabele" IS NOT NULL
  ),
  init AS (
    SELECT
      grp,
      array_agg(klub_id ORDER BY rn)::int[] AS arr,
      COUNT(*)::int AS n
    FROM teams
    GROUP BY grp
  ),
  rounds AS (
    -- start: r=1 za SVAKU grupu
    SELECT grp, 1 AS r, arr, n
    FROM init
    UNION ALL
    -- rotacija (circle method): fix arr[1], rotiraj ostalo
    SELECT
      grp,
      r + 1,
      (arr[1:1] || arr[n:n] || arr[2:n-1])::int[],
      n
    FROM rounds
    WHERE r < (SELECT n - 1 FROM init i WHERE i.grp = rounds.grp)
  ),
  pairs_first_leg AS (
    SELECT
      ro.grp,
      ro.r,
      i,
      CASE WHEN (ro.r + i) % 2 = 0 THEN ro.arr[i] ELSE ro.arr[ro.n+1-i] END AS home_id,
      CASE WHEN (ro.r + i) % 2 = 0 THEN ro.arr[ro.n+1-i] ELSE ro.arr[i] END AS away_id
    FROM rounds ro
    CROSS JOIN LATERAL generate_series(1, ro.n/2) AS i
  ),
  pairs_all AS (
    -- prva polusezona
    SELECT grp, r, home_id, away_id
    FROM pairs_first_leg
    UNION ALL
    -- revanši: zameni domaćin/gost, r pomeri za (n-1)
    SELECT
      p.grp,
      p.r + (SELECT i.n - 1 FROM init i WHERE i.grp = p.grp) AS r,
      p.away_id AS home_id,
      p.home_id AS away_id
    FROM pairs_first_leg p
  ),
  pair_names AS (
    SELECT
      p.grp,
      p.r,
      kh."Naziv" AS domacin,
      kg."Naziv" AS gost
    FROM pairs_all p
    JOIN "Klub" kh ON kh."Id" = p.home_id
    JOIN "Klub" kg ON kg."Id" = p.away_id
  ),
  kolodata AS (
    SELECT
      k."Id" AS kolo_id,
      k."BrojKola" AS r,
      k."PocetakKola" AS poc,
      k."KrajKola" AS kraj
    FROM "Kolo" k
    WHERE k."TakmicenjeId" = v_takmicenje_id
      AND k."TipKola" = 1
  )
  SELECT
    (v_base_ut + row_number() OVER (ORDER BY pn.grp, pn.r, pn.domacin, pn.gost)) AS utakmica_id,
    (v_base_st + row_number() OVER (ORDER BY pn.grp, pn.r, pn.domacin, pn.gost)) AS statistika_id,
    pn.grp,
    pn.domacin,
    pn.gost,
    kd.kolo_id,
    -- datum utakmice RANDOM unutar [PocetakKola, KrajKola]
    (kd.poc + (random() * (kd.kraj - kd.poc))) AS datum_ts
  FROM pair_names pn
  JOIN kolodata kd ON kd.r = pn.r;

  -- 4) UBACI UTAKMICE
  INSERT INTO "Utakmica"
  (
    "Id","Uzivo","Domacin","Gost","Lokacija","Rezultat",
    "KoloId","StatistikaId","DatumPocetkaUtakmice"
  )
  SELECT
    s.utakmica_id,
    CASE WHEN s.datum_ts::date = CURRENT_DATE THEN TRUE ELSE FALSE END,
    s.domacin,
    s.gost,
    'Hala ' || s.domacin,
    '0:0',
    s.kolo_id,
    NULL,
    s.datum_ts
  FROM tmp_schedule s
  ORDER BY s.utakmica_id;

  -- 5) UBACI KOŠARKA STATISTIKE + ASISTENCIJE
  -- (popuni samo košarka kolone + asistencije; ostale ostaju NULL)
  INSERT INTO "Statistika"
  (
    "Id",
    "TrenutniMinut",
    "UtakmicaId",
    "Sport",

    "PrvaCetDomacin","PrvaCetGost",
    "DrugaCetDomacin","DrugaCetGost",
    "TrecaCetDomacin","TrecaCetGost",
    "CetvCetDomacin","CetvCetGost",

    "TwoPointDomacin","TwoPointGost",
    "ThreePointDomacin","ThreePointGost",
    "FreeThrowDomacin","FreeThrowGost",

    "ReboundsDomacin","ReboundsGost",
    "StealsDomacin","StealsGost",
    "BlocksDomacin","BlocksGost",

    "AsistencijeDomacin","AsistencijeGost"
  )
  SELECT
    s.statistika_id,
    CASE
      WHEN s.datum_ts::date < CURRENT_DATE THEN 40
      WHEN s.datum_ts::date > CURRENT_DATE THEN 0
      ELSE (10 + (s.utakmica_id % 28)) -- "live" minut simulacija
    END,
    s.utakmica_id,
    2,

    -- četvrtine (realističnije: 15-30 po četvrtini za odigrane, 0 za buduće)
    CASE WHEN s.datum_ts::date > CURRENT_DATE THEN 0 ELSE (15 + (s.utakmica_id % 16)) END,
    CASE WHEN s.datum_ts::date > CURRENT_DATE THEN 0 ELSE (15 + ((s.utakmica_id+3) % 16)) END,

    CASE WHEN s.datum_ts::date > CURRENT_DATE THEN 0 ELSE (15 + ((s.utakmica_id+1) % 16)) END,
    CASE WHEN s.datum_ts::date > CURRENT_DATE THEN 0 ELSE (15 + ((s.utakmica_id+4) % 16)) END,

    CASE WHEN s.datum_ts::date > CURRENT_DATE THEN 0 ELSE (15 + ((s.utakmica_id+2) % 16)) END,
    CASE WHEN s.datum_ts::date > CURRENT_DATE THEN 0 ELSE (15 + ((s.utakmica_id+5) % 16)) END,

    CASE WHEN s.datum_ts::date > CURRENT_DATE THEN 0 ELSE (15 + ((s.utakmica_id+6) % 16)) END,
    CASE WHEN s.datum_ts::date > CURRENT_DATE THEN 0 ELSE (15 + ((s.utakmica_id+7) % 16)) END,

    -- šutevi (pogodjeni)
    CASE WHEN s.datum_ts::date > CURRENT_DATE THEN 0 ELSE (18 + (s.utakmica_id % 14)) END,
    CASE WHEN s.datum_ts::date > CURRENT_DATE THEN 0 ELSE (18 + ((s.utakmica_id+2) % 14)) END,

    CASE WHEN s.datum_ts::date > CURRENT_DATE THEN 0 ELSE (6 + (s.utakmica_id % 10)) END,
    CASE WHEN s.datum_ts::date > CURRENT_DATE THEN 0 ELSE (6 + ((s.utakmica_id+2) % 10)) END,

    CASE WHEN s.datum_ts::date > CURRENT_DATE THEN 0 ELSE (10 + (s.utakmica_id % 12)) END,
    CASE WHEN s.datum_ts::date > CURRENT_DATE THEN 0 ELSE (10 + ((s.utakmica_id+2) % 12)) END,

    -- boxscore
    CASE WHEN s.datum_ts::date > CURRENT_DATE THEN 0 ELSE (28 + (s.utakmica_id % 18)) END,
    CASE WHEN s.datum_ts::date > CURRENT_DATE THEN 0 ELSE (28 + ((s.utakmica_id+5) % 18)) END,

    CASE WHEN s.datum_ts::date > CURRENT_DATE THEN 0 ELSE (4 + (s.utakmica_id % 11)) END,
    CASE WHEN s.datum_ts::date > CURRENT_DATE THEN 0 ELSE (4 + ((s.utakmica_id+2) % 11)) END,

    CASE WHEN s.datum_ts::date > CURRENT_DATE THEN 0 ELSE (1 + (s.utakmica_id % 8)) END,
    CASE WHEN s.datum_ts::date > CURRENT_DATE THEN 0 ELSE (1 + ((s.utakmica_id+4) % 8)) END,

    -- asistencije (košarka: tipično 10-30)
    CASE WHEN s.datum_ts::date > CURRENT_DATE THEN 0 ELSE (10 + (s.utakmica_id % 21)) END,
    CASE WHEN s.datum_ts::date > CURRENT_DATE THEN 0 ELSE (10 + ((s.utakmica_id+7) % 21)) END
  FROM tmp_schedule s
  ORDER BY s.statistika_id;

  -- 6) VEŽI utakmice -> statistike
  UPDATE "Utakmica" u
  SET "StatistikaId" = s.statistika_id
  FROM tmp_schedule s
  WHERE u."Id" = s.utakmica_id;

  -- 7) UPDATE Rezultat iz četvrtina (samo za odigrane i live)
  UPDATE "Utakmica" u
  SET "Rezultat" =
    (COALESCE(st."PrvaCetDomacin",0) + COALESCE(st."DrugaCetDomacin",0) +
     COALESCE(st."TrecaCetDomacin",0) + COALESCE(st."CetvCetDomacin",0))::text
    || ':' ||
    (COALESCE(st."PrvaCetGost",0) + COALESCE(st."DrugaCetGost",0) +
     COALESCE(st."TrecaCetGost",0) + COALESCE(st."CetvCetGost",0))::text
  FROM "Statistika" st, tmp_schedule s
  WHERE u."Id" = s.utakmica_id
    AND st."Id" = s.statistika_id
    AND s.datum_ts::date <= CURRENT_DATE;

  -- 8) Vrati NOT NULL
  ALTER TABLE "Utakmica" ALTER COLUMN "StatistikaId" SET NOT NULL;

END $$;

COMMIT;

-- brza provera: broj utakmica po kolu (tip=1) i grupama (vidi iz Domacin/Gost naziva + Tabela)
SELECT k."BrojKola", COUNT(*) AS utakmica_u_kolu
FROM "Utakmica" u
JOIN "Kolo" k ON k."Id" = u."KoloId"
WHERE k."TakmicenjeId" = 10 AND k."TipKola" = 1
GROUP BY k."BrojKola"
ORDER BY k."BrojKola";
-- DODAVANJE UTAKMICA SA STATISTIKOM ZA NBA
BEGIN;

DO $$
DECLARE
  v_takmicenje_id int := 11;

  v_base_ut int;
  v_base_st int;

  v_set_sql text;
BEGIN
  -- Ako je StatistikaId NOT NULL u Utakmica
  ALTER TABLE "Utakmica" ALTER COLUMN "StatistikaId" DROP NOT NULL;

  SELECT COALESCE(MAX("Id"),0) INTO v_base_ut FROM "Utakmica";
  SELECT COALESCE(MAX("Id"),0) INTO v_base_st FROM "Statistika";

  DROP TABLE IF EXISTS tmp_games;

  CREATE TEMP TABLE tmp_games AS
  WITH teams AS (
    SELECT t."KlubId", t."NazivTabele", k."Naziv"
    FROM "Tabela" t
    JOIN "Klub" k ON k."Id" = t."KlubId"
    WHERE t."TakmicenjeId" = v_takmicenje_id
  ),
  pairs AS (
    -- EAST-EAST (4)
    SELECT a."KlubId" h, b."KlubId" g, 4 cnt
    FROM teams a JOIN teams b ON a."KlubId" < b."KlubId"
    WHERE a."NazivTabele"='NBA-EAST' AND b."NazivTabele"='NBA-EAST'

    UNION ALL
    -- WEST-WEST (4)
    SELECT a."KlubId", b."KlubId", 4
    FROM teams a JOIN teams b ON a."KlubId" < b."KlubId"
    WHERE a."NazivTabele"='NBA-WEST' AND b."NazivTabele"='NBA-WEST'

    UNION ALL
    -- EAST-WEST (2)
    SELECT a."KlubId", b."KlubId", 2
    FROM teams a JOIN teams b
    ON a."NazivTabele"='NBA-EAST' AND b."NazivTabele"='NBA-WEST'
  ),
  expanded AS (
    SELECT h, g, generate_series(1,cnt) n FROM pairs
  ),
  ha AS (
    SELECT
      CASE WHEN n%2=1 THEN h ELSE g END home_id,
      CASE WHEN n%2=1 THEN g ELSE h END away_id
    FROM expanded
  ),
  numbered AS (
    SELECT *, row_number() OVER() rn FROM ha
  ),
  kola AS (
    SELECT "Id","PocetakKola","KrajKola",
           row_number() OVER(ORDER BY "BrojKola") r
    FROM "Kolo"
    WHERE "TakmicenjeId"=v_takmicenje_id AND "TipKola"=1
  )
  SELECT
    v_base_ut + rn AS utakmica_id,
    v_base_st + rn AS statistika_id,
    kh."Naziv" AS domacin,
    kg."Naziv" AS gost,
    k."Id" AS kolo_id,
    (k."PocetakKola" + random()*(k."KrajKola"-k."PocetakKola")) AS datum_ts
  FROM numbered n
  JOIN "Klub" kh ON kh."Id"=n.home_id
  JOIN "Klub" kg ON kg."Id"=n.away_id
  JOIN kola k ON k.r=((n.rn-1)%82)+1;

  -- 1) UTKMICE
  INSERT INTO "Utakmica"
  ("Id","Uzivo","Domacin","Gost","Lokacija","Rezultat","KoloId","StatistikaId","DatumPocetkaUtakmice")
  SELECT
    utakmica_id,
    (datum_ts::date = CURRENT_DATE),
    domacin,
    gost,
    'NBA Arena',
    '0:0',
    kolo_id,
    statistika_id,
    datum_ts
  FROM tmp_games;

  -- 2) STATISTIKA (minimum koji znamo)
  INSERT INTO "Statistika"
  (
    "Id","UtakmicaId","Sport","TrenutniMinut",
    "PrvaCetDomacin","DrugaCetDomacin","TrecaCetDomacin","CetvCetDomacin",
    "PrvaCetGost","DrugaCetGost","TrecaCetGost","CetvCetGost"
  )
  SELECT
    statistika_id,
    utakmica_id,
    2,
    CASE WHEN datum_ts::date < CURRENT_DATE THEN 48 ELSE 0 END,

    -- kvartovi: odigrane random, buduće 0
    CASE WHEN datum_ts::date < CURRENT_DATE THEN 20+(random()*16)::int ELSE 0 END,
    CASE WHEN datum_ts::date < CURRENT_DATE THEN 20+(random()*16)::int ELSE 0 END,
    CASE WHEN datum_ts::date < CURRENT_DATE THEN 20+(random()*16)::int ELSE 0 END,
    CASE WHEN datum_ts::date < CURRENT_DATE THEN 20+(random()*16)::int ELSE 0 END,

    CASE WHEN datum_ts::date < CURRENT_DATE THEN 20+(random()*16)::int ELSE 0 END,
    CASE WHEN datum_ts::date < CURRENT_DATE THEN 20+(random()*16)::int ELSE 0 END,
    CASE WHEN datum_ts::date < CURRENT_DATE THEN 20+(random()*16)::int ELSE 0 END,
    CASE WHEN datum_ts::date < CURRENT_DATE THEN 20+(random()*16)::int ELSE 0 END
  FROM tmp_games;

  /*
    3) Popuni SVA ostala numerička košarkaška polja:
       - buduće utakmice: 0
       - odigrane: realni rasponi (heuristika po nazivu kolone)
       - ništa ne ostaje NULL
  */
  SELECT string_agg(
    format(
      '%1$I = COALESCE(%2$s, 0)',
      a.attname,
      CASE
        WHEN lower(a.attname) IN (
          'id','utakmicaid','sport','trenutniminut',
          'prvacetdomacin','drugacetdomacin','trecacetdomacin','cetvcetdomacin',
          'prvacetgost','drugacetgost','trecacetgost','cetvcetgost'
        )
        THEN format('s.%I', a.attname)

        ELSE
          -- Ako je ODIGRANO => random realno; ako NIJE => 0
          format(
            'CASE WHEN u."DatumPocetkaUtakmice"::date < CURRENT_DATE THEN %s ELSE 0 END',
            CASE
              -- asistencije 18-34
              WHEN lower(a.attname) LIKE '%asistencij%domacin%' OR lower(a.attname) LIKE '%assist%domacin%' THEN '(18 + (random()*17)::int)'
              WHEN lower(a.attname) LIKE '%asistencij%gost%'    OR lower(a.attname) LIKE '%assist%gost%'    THEN '(18 + (random()*17)::int)'

              -- skokovi 35-60
              WHEN lower(a.attname) LIKE '%skok%domacin%' OR lower(a.attname) LIKE '%rebound%domacin%' THEN '(35 + (random()*26)::int)'
              WHEN lower(a.attname) LIKE '%skok%gost%'    OR lower(a.attname) LIKE '%rebound%gost%'    THEN '(35 + (random()*26)::int)'

              -- ofanzivni skokovi 6-18
              WHEN lower(a.attname) LIKE '%ofanz%skok%domacin%' OR lower(a.attname) LIKE '%off%rebound%domacin%' THEN '(6 + (random()*13)::int)'
              WHEN lower(a.attname) LIKE '%ofanz%skok%gost%'    OR lower(a.attname) LIKE '%off%rebound%gost%'    THEN '(6 + (random()*13)::int)'

              -- defanzivni skokovi 22-45
              WHEN lower(a.attname) LIKE '%defanz%skok%domacin%' OR lower(a.attname) LIKE '%def%rebound%domacin%' THEN '(22 + (random()*24)::int)'
              WHEN lower(a.attname) LIKE '%defanz%skok%gost%'    OR lower(a.attname) LIKE '%def%rebound%gost%'    THEN '(22 + (random()*24)::int)'

              -- ukradene 4-12
              WHEN lower(a.attname) LIKE '%ukrad%domacin%' OR lower(a.attname) LIKE '%steal%domacin%' THEN '(4 + (random()*9)::int)'
              WHEN lower(a.attname) LIKE '%ukrad%gost%'    OR lower(a.attname) LIKE '%steal%gost%'    THEN '(4 + (random()*9)::int)'

              -- blokade 2-9
              WHEN lower(a.attname) LIKE '%blok%domacin%' OR lower(a.attname) LIKE '%block%domacin%' THEN '(2 + (random()*8)::int)'
              WHEN lower(a.attname) LIKE '%blok%gost%'    OR lower(a.attname) LIKE '%block%gost%'    THEN '(2 + (random()*8)::int)'

              -- izgubljene 9-18
              WHEN lower(a.attname) LIKE '%izgubl%domacin%' OR lower(a.attname) LIKE '%turnover%domacin%' THEN '(9 + (random()*10)::int)'
              WHEN lower(a.attname) LIKE '%izgubl%gost%'    OR lower(a.attname) LIKE '%turnover%gost%'    THEN '(9 + (random()*10)::int)'

              -- faulovi 15-25
              WHEN lower(a.attname) LIKE '%faul%domacin%' OR lower(a.attname) LIKE '%gresk%domacin%' OR lower(a.attname) LIKE '%foul%domacin%' THEN '(15 + (random()*11)::int)'
              WHEN lower(a.attname) LIKE '%faul%gost%'    OR lower(a.attname) LIKE '%gresk%gost%'    OR lower(a.attname) LIKE '%foul%gost%'    THEN '(15 + (random()*11)::int)'

              -- 3PT pogodjeni 7-18, pokusaji 22-45
              WHEN lower(a.attname) LIKE '%3%pogo%domacin%' OR lower(a.attname) LIKE '%3pt%made%domacin%' OR lower(a.attname) LIKE '%trojk%pogo%domacin%' THEN '(7 + (random()*12)::int)'
              WHEN lower(a.attname) LIKE '%3%pogo%gost%'    OR lower(a.attname) LIKE '%3pt%made%gost%'    OR lower(a.attname) LIKE '%trojk%pogo%gost%'    THEN '(7 + (random()*12)::int)'

              WHEN lower(a.attname) LIKE '%3%poku%domacin%' OR lower(a.attname) LIKE '%3pt%att%domacin%' OR lower(a.attname) LIKE '%trojk%poku%domacin%' THEN '(22 + (random()*24)::int)'
              WHEN lower(a.attname) LIKE '%3%poku%gost%'    OR lower(a.attname) LIKE '%3pt%att%gost%'    OR lower(a.attname) LIKE '%trojk%poku%gost%'    THEN '(22 + (random()*24)::int)'

              -- slobodna pogodjena 14-26, pokusaji 18-33
              WHEN lower(a.attname) LIKE '%slobod%pogo%domacin%' OR lower(a.attname) LIKE '%ft%made%domacin%' THEN '(14 + (random()*13)::int)'
              WHEN lower(a.attname) LIKE '%slobod%pogo%gost%'    OR lower(a.attname) LIKE '%ft%made%gost%'    THEN '(14 + (random()*13)::int)'

              WHEN lower(a.attname) LIKE '%slobod%poku%domacin%' OR lower(a.attname) LIKE '%ft%att%domacin%' THEN '(18 + (random()*16)::int)'
              WHEN lower(a.attname) LIKE '%slobod%poku%gost%'    OR lower(a.attname) LIKE '%ft%att%gost%'    THEN '(18 + (random()*16)::int)'

              -- FG pogodjeni 35-48, pokusaji 75-98
              WHEN lower(a.attname) LIKE '%sut%pogo%domacin%' OR lower(a.attname) LIKE '%fg%made%domacin%' OR lower(a.attname) LIKE '%field%made%domacin%' THEN '(35 + (random()*14)::int)'
              WHEN lower(a.attname) LIKE '%sut%pogo%gost%'    OR lower(a.attname) LIKE '%fg%made%gost%'    OR lower(a.attname) LIKE '%field%made%gost%'    THEN '(35 + (random()*14)::int)'

              WHEN lower(a.attname) LIKE '%sut%poku%domacin%' OR lower(a.attname) LIKE '%fg%att%domacin%' OR lower(a.attname) LIKE '%field%att%domacin%' THEN '(75 + (random()*24)::int)'
              WHEN lower(a.attname) LIKE '%sut%poku%gost%'    OR lower(a.attname) LIKE '%fg%att%gost%'    OR lower(a.attname) LIKE '%field%att%gost%'    THEN '(75 + (random()*24)::int)'

              -- poeni sa klupe 25-55
              WHEN lower(a.attname) LIKE '%klup%domacin%' OR lower(a.attname) LIKE '%bench%domacin%' THEN '(25 + (random()*31)::int)'
              WHEN lower(a.attname) LIKE '%klup%gost%'    OR lower(a.attname) LIKE '%bench%gost%'    THEN '(25 + (random()*31)::int)'

              -- generički: numeričko team stat polje 0-40 (bolje nego sve 0)
              WHEN lower(a.attname) LIKE '%domacin%' OR lower(a.attname) LIKE '%gost%' THEN '((random()*41)::int)'

              -- sve ostalo numeričko: 0-20
              ELSE '((random()*21)::int)'
            END
          )
      END
    ),
    ', '
  )
  INTO v_set_sql
  FROM pg_attribute a
  JOIN pg_class c ON c.oid = a.attrelid
  JOIN pg_namespace n ON n.oid = c.relnamespace
  WHERE n.nspname = 'public'
    AND c.relname = 'Statistika'
    AND a.attnum > 0
    AND NOT a.attisdropped
    AND a.atttypid IN (
      'int2'::regtype, 'int4'::regtype, 'int8'::regtype,
      'numeric'::regtype, 'float4'::regtype, 'float8'::regtype
    );

  IF v_set_sql IS NOT NULL THEN
    EXECUTE format(
      'UPDATE "Statistika" s
       SET %s
       FROM "Utakmica" u
       WHERE u."StatistikaId" = s."Id"
         AND s."Sport" = 2
         AND s."Id" IN (SELECT statistika_id FROM tmp_games);',
      v_set_sql
    );
  END IF;

  -- 4) Vrati NOT NULL constraint nazad
  ALTER TABLE "Utakmica" ALTER COLUMN "StatistikaId" SET NOT NULL;

END $$;

COMMIT;

-- PROVERA: Utakmica bez StatistikaId
SELECT COUNT(*)
FROM "Utakmica" u
LEFT JOIN "Statistika" s ON s."Id"=u."StatistikaId"
WHERE u."StatistikaId" IS NULL;

-- UPDATE REZULTATA: zbir četvrtina, format "domacin:gost"
UPDATE "Utakmica" u
SET "Rezultat" =
  (COALESCE(st."PrvaCetDomacin",0)
 + COALESCE(st."DrugaCetDomacin",0)
 + COALESCE(st."TrecaCetDomacin",0)
 + COALESCE(st."CetvCetDomacin",0))::text
 || ':' ||
  (COALESCE(st."PrvaCetGost",0)
 + COALESCE(st."DrugaCetGost",0)
 + COALESCE(st."TrecaCetGost",0)
 + COALESCE(st."CetvCetGost",0))::text
FROM "Statistika" st
WHERE u."StatistikaId" = st."Id";
-----------------------------------
DODAVANJE UTAKMICE SA STATISTIKOM ZA VATERPOLO LIGU SAMPIONA
------------------------------------------------------------


BEGIN;

DO $$
DECLARE
  v_takmicenje_id int := 12;  -- PROMENI na 12/13/14
  v_sezona text := '2025/26';
  v_base_ut int;
  v_base_st int;
  v_current_ts timestamp := NOW();
  rec RECORD;
BEGIN
  ALTER TABLE "Utakmica" ALTER COLUMN "StatistikaId" DROP NOT NULL;

  DELETE FROM "Statistika" s
  USING "Utakmica" u, "Kolo" k
  WHERE s."UtakmicaId" = u."Id"
    AND u."KoloId" = k."Id"
    AND k."TakmicenjeId" = v_takmicenje_id;

  DELETE FROM "Utakmica" u
  USING "Kolo" k
  WHERE u."KoloId" = k."Id"
    AND k."TakmicenjeId" = v_takmicenje_id;

  SELECT COALESCE(MAX("Id"),0) INTO v_base_ut FROM "Utakmica";
  SELECT COALESCE(MAX("Id"),0) INTO v_base_st FROM "Statistika";

  DROP TABLE IF EXISTS tmp_schedule;

  CREATE TEMP TABLE tmp_schedule AS
  WITH teams AS (
    SELECT
      RIGHT(TRIM(t."NazivTabele"), 1) AS grp,
      t."KlubId",
      ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY RIGHT(TRIM(t."NazivTabele"), 1) ORDER BY t."KlubId") AS rn
    FROM "Tabela" t
    WHERE t."TakmicenjeId" = v_takmicenje_id
      AND t."Sezona" = v_sezona
      AND t."NazivTabele" IS NOT NULL
      AND t."NazivTabele" LIKE '%Group%'
  ),
  group_size AS (
    SELECT grp, COUNT(*) as n
    FROM teams
    GROUP BY grp
  ),
  pairs_per_group AS (
    SELECT
      a.grp,
      a."KlubId" AS home_id,
      b."KlubId" AS away_id,
      1 + ((ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY a.grp ORDER BY a."KlubId", b."KlubId") - 1) 
           % (SELECT n-1 FROM group_size gs WHERE gs.grp = a.grp)) AS group_round
    FROM teams a
    JOIN teams b ON a.grp = b.grp AND a.rn < b.rn
  ),
  all_games AS (
    SELECT grp, home_id, away_id, group_round FROM pairs_per_group
    UNION ALL
    SELECT 
      grp, 
      away_id AS home_id, 
      home_id AS away_id,
      group_round + (SELECT MAX(n-1) FROM group_size WHERE grp = pairs_per_group.grp) AS group_round
    FROM pairs_per_group
  ),
  kola AS (
    SELECT
      "Id" AS kolo_id,
      "BrojKola",
      "PocetakKola" AS poc,
      "KrajKola" AS kraj,
      ROW_NUMBER() OVER (ORDER BY "BrojKola") AS kolo_seq
    FROM "Kolo"
    WHERE "TakmicenjeId" = v_takmicenje_id
      AND "TipKola" = 1
      AND "Sezona" = v_sezona
    ORDER BY "BrojKola"
  )
  SELECT
    v_base_ut + ROW_NUMBER() OVER (ORDER BY ag.group_round, ag.grp, ag.home_id) AS utakmica_id,
    v_base_st + ROW_NUMBER() OVER (ORDER BY ag.group_round, ag.grp, ag.home_id) AS statistika_id,
    ag.grp,
    kh."Naziv" AS domacin,
    kg."Naziv" AS gost,
    k.kolo_id,
    k."BrojKola",
    ag.group_round,
    (k.poc + random()*(k.kraj-k.poc)) AS datum_ts,
    random() AS seed
  FROM all_games ag
  JOIN "Klub" kh ON kh."Id" = ag.home_id
  JOIN "Klub" kg ON kg."Id" = ag.away_id
  JOIN kola k ON k.kolo_seq = ag.group_round;

  RAISE NOTICE '=== PROVERA RASPOREDA ===';
  FOR rec IN 
    SELECT 
      "BrojKola",
      COUNT(*) FILTER (WHERE grp = 'A') as grp_a,
      COUNT(*) FILTER (WHERE grp = 'B') as grp_b,
      COUNT(*) FILTER (WHERE grp = 'C') as grp_c,
      COUNT(*) FILTER (WHERE grp = 'D') as grp_d,
      COUNT(*) as total
    FROM tmp_schedule
    GROUP BY "BrojKola"
    ORDER BY "BrojKola"
  LOOP
    RAISE NOTICE 'Kolo %: A=%, B=%, C=%, D=%, Ukupno=%',
      rec."BrojKola", 
      COALESCE(rec.grp_a, 0),
      COALESCE(rec.grp_b, 0),
      COALESCE(rec.grp_c, 0),
      COALESCE(rec.grp_d, 0),
      rec.total;
  END LOOP;

  INSERT INTO "Utakmica"
  ("Id","Uzivo","Domacin","Gost","Lokacija","Rezultat","KoloId","StatistikaId","DatumPocetkaUtakmice")
  SELECT
    s.utakmica_id,
    CASE 
      WHEN s.datum_ts <= v_current_ts 
       AND s.datum_ts + INTERVAL '32 minutes' > v_current_ts 
      THEN TRUE 
      ELSE FALSE 
    END,
    s.domacin,
    s.gost,
    'Bazen ' || s.domacin,
    '0:0',
    s.kolo_id,
    NULL,
    s.datum_ts
  FROM tmp_schedule s;

  -- ✅ ISPRAVLJENA STATISTIKA - jedan LATERAL za četvrtine
  INSERT INTO "Statistika"
  (
    "Id", "UtakmicaId", "Sport", "TrenutniMinut",
    "GoloviDomacin", "GoloviGost",
    "SutDomacin", "SutGost",
    "SutKaGolDomacin", "SutKaGolGost",
    "VP_PrvaCetDomacin", "VP_DrugaCetDomacin", "VP_TrecaCetDomacin", "VP_CetvCetDomacin",
    "VP_PrvaCetGost", "VP_DrugaCetGost", "VP_TrecaCetGost", "VP_CetvCetGost",
    "IskljucenjaDomacin", "IskljucenjaGost",
    "PeterciDomacin", "PeterciGost",
    "AsistencijeDomacin", "AsistencijeGost",
    "ListaStrelaca"
  )
  SELECT
    s.statistika_id, s.utakmica_id, 3,
    
    CASE
      WHEN s.datum_ts > v_current_ts THEN 0
      WHEN s.datum_ts <= v_current_ts 
       AND s.datum_ts + INTERVAL '32 minutes' > v_current_ts 
      THEN LEAST(EXTRACT(EPOCH FROM (v_current_ts - s.datum_ts))::int / 60, 32)
      ELSE 32
    END,
    
    floor(gd_full * min_factor)::int,
    floor(gg_full * min_factor)::int,
    
    floor(sut_d_full * min_factor)::int,
    floor(sut_g_full * min_factor)::int,
    floor(sut_ka_d_full * min_factor)::int,
    floor(sut_ka_g_full * min_factor)::int,
    
    floor(q.cet1_d * min_factor)::int,
    floor(q.cet2_d * min_factor)::int,
    floor(q.cet3_d * min_factor)::int,
    floor(q.cet4_d * min_factor)::int,
    
    floor(q.cet1_g * min_factor)::int,
    floor(q.cet2_g * min_factor)::int,
    floor(q.cet3_g * min_factor)::int,
    floor(q.cet4_g * min_factor)::int,
    
    floor(iskl_d_full * min_factor)::int,
    floor(iskl_g_full * min_factor)::int,
    
    floor(pet_d_full * min_factor)::int,
    floor(pet_g_full * min_factor)::int,
    
    floor(asist_d_full * min_factor)::int,
    floor(asist_g_full * min_factor)::int,
    
    NULL::text
    
  FROM tmp_schedule s
  CROSS JOIN LATERAL (
    SELECT
      CASE
        WHEN s.datum_ts > v_current_ts THEN 0.0
        WHEN s.datum_ts <= v_current_ts 
         AND s.datum_ts + INTERVAL '32 minutes' > v_current_ts 
        THEN LEAST(EXTRACT(EPOCH FROM (v_current_ts - s.datum_ts)) / (32.0 * 60), 1.0)
        ELSE 1.0
      END AS min_factor
  ) factor
  CROSS JOIN LATERAL (
    SELECT
      (7 + floor((s.seed + random()) * 11))::int AS gd_full,
      (5 + floor((s.seed + random()) * 10))::int AS gg_full,
      
      (20 + floor((s.seed + random()) * 20))::int AS sut_d_full,
      (18 + floor((s.seed + random()) * 18))::int AS sut_g_full,
      
      (2 + floor((s.seed + random()) * 9))::int AS sut_ka_d_full,
      (2 + floor((s.seed + random()) * 8))::int AS sut_ka_g_full,
      
      (1 + floor((s.seed + random()) * 9))::int AS iskl_d_full,
      (1 + floor((s.seed + random()) * 9))::int AS iskl_g_full,
      
      floor((s.seed + random()) * 4)::int AS pet_d_full,
      floor((s.seed + random()) * 4)::int AS pet_g_full,
      
      (1 + floor((s.seed + random()) * 11))::int AS asist_d_full,
      (1 + floor((s.seed + random()) * 10))::int AS asist_g_full
  ) stats_full
  CROSS JOIN LATERAL (
    -- ✅ SVE četvrtine u jednom LATERAL bloku
    SELECT
      (1 + floor((s.seed + random()) * (gd_full * 0.35)))::int AS c1d,
      (1 + floor((s.seed + random()) * (gd_full * 0.35)))::int AS c2d,
      (floor((s.seed + random()) * (gd_full * 0.30)))::int AS c3d,
      
      (1 + floor((s.seed + random()) * (gg_full * 0.35)))::int AS c1g,
      (1 + floor((s.seed + random()) * (gg_full * 0.35)))::int AS c2g,
      (floor((s.seed + random()) * (gg_full * 0.30)))::int AS c3g
  ) quarters_temp
  CROSS JOIN LATERAL (
    -- Računaj četvrtu četvrtinu kao ostatak
    SELECT
      c1d AS cet1_d,
      c2d AS cet2_d,
      c3d AS cet3_d,
      GREATEST(0, gd_full - c1d - c2d - c3d) AS cet4_d,
      
      c1g AS cet1_g,
      c2g AS cet2_g,
      c3g AS cet3_g,
      GREATEST(0, gg_full - c1g - c2g - c3g) AS cet4_g
  ) q;

  UPDATE "Utakmica" u
  SET "StatistikaId" = s.statistika_id
  FROM tmp_schedule s
  WHERE u."Id" = s.utakmica_id;

  UPDATE "Utakmica" u
  SET "Rezultat" =
    (st."VP_PrvaCetDomacin" + st."VP_DrugaCetDomacin" + 
     st."VP_TrecaCetDomacin" + st."VP_CetvCetDomacin")::text
    || ':' ||
    (st."VP_PrvaCetGost" + st."VP_DrugaCetGost" + 
     st."VP_TrecaCetGost" + st."VP_CetvCetGost")::text
  FROM "Statistika" st
  WHERE u."StatistikaId" = st."Id"
    AND st."Sport" = 3;

  ALTER TABLE "Utakmica" ALTER COLUMN "StatistikaId" SET NOT NULL;

  RAISE NOTICE '';
  RAISE NOTICE '=== STATUS UTAKMICA ===';
  FOR rec IN
    SELECT
      CASE 
        WHEN datum_ts > v_current_ts THEN 'Buduće'
        WHEN datum_ts <= v_current_ts 
         AND datum_ts + INTERVAL '32 minutes' > v_current_ts 
        THEN 'Uživo'
        ELSE 'Završene'
      END AS status,
      COUNT(*) as br
    FROM tmp_schedule
    GROUP BY 
      CASE 
        WHEN datum_ts > v_current_ts THEN 'Buduće'
        WHEN datum_ts <= v_current_ts 
         AND datum_ts + INTERVAL '32 minutes' > v_current_ts 
        THEN 'Uživo'
        ELSE 'Završene'
      END
  LOOP
    RAISE NOTICE '%: % utakmica', rec.status, rec.br;
  END LOOP;

  RAISE NOTICE '';
  RAISE NOTICE '=== ZAVRŠENO ===';
  RAISE NOTICE 'Ukupno: % utakmica', (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM tmp_schedule);

END $$;

COMMIT;


-----------------------------------------------------------------
DODAVANJE UTAKMICA SA STATISTIKOM ZA VATERPOLO EURO CUP
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
BEGIN;

DO $$
DECLARE
  v_takmicenje_id int := 13;  -- PROMENI na 12/13/14
  v_sezona text := '2025/26';
  v_base_ut int;
  v_base_st int;
  v_current_ts timestamp := NOW();
  rec RECORD;  -- ✅ Dodao DECLARE za rec
BEGIN
  ALTER TABLE "Utakmica" ALTER COLUMN "StatistikaId" DROP NOT NULL;

  -- Brisanje starih podataka
  DELETE FROM "Statistika" s
  USING "Utakmica" u, "Kolo" k
  WHERE s."UtakmicaId" = u."Id"
    AND u."KoloId" = k."Id"
    AND k."TakmicenjeId" = v_takmicenje_id;

  DELETE FROM "Utakmica" u
  USING "Kolo" k
  WHERE u."KoloId" = k."Id"
    AND k."TakmicenjeId" = v_takmicenje_id;

  SELECT COALESCE(MAX("Id"),0) INTO v_base_ut FROM "Utakmica";
  SELECT COALESCE(MAX("Id"),0) INTO v_base_st FROM "Statistika";

  DROP TABLE IF EXISTS tmp_schedule;

  -- Raspored sa grupama
  CREATE TEMP TABLE tmp_schedule AS
  WITH teams AS (
    SELECT
      RIGHT(TRIM(t."NazivTabele"), 1) AS grp,
      t."KlubId",
      ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY RIGHT(TRIM(t."NazivTabele"), 1) ORDER BY t."KlubId") AS rn
    FROM "Tabela" t
    WHERE t."TakmicenjeId" = v_takmicenje_id
      AND t."Sezona" = v_sezona
      AND t."NazivTabele" IS NOT NULL
      AND t."NazivTabele" LIKE '%Group%'
  ),
  group_size AS (
    SELECT grp, COUNT(*) as n
    FROM teams
    GROUP BY grp
  ),
  pairs_per_group AS (
    SELECT
      a.grp,
      a."KlubId" AS home_id,
      b."KlubId" AS away_id,
      1 + ((ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY a.grp ORDER BY a."KlubId", b."KlubId") - 1) 
           % (SELECT n-1 FROM group_size gs WHERE gs.grp = a.grp)) AS group_round
    FROM teams a
    JOIN teams b ON a.grp = b.grp AND a.rn < b.rn
  ),
  all_games AS (
    SELECT grp, home_id, away_id, group_round FROM pairs_per_group
    UNION ALL
    SELECT 
      grp, 
      away_id AS home_id, 
      home_id AS away_id,
      group_round + (SELECT MAX(n-1) FROM group_size WHERE grp = pairs_per_group.grp) AS group_round
    FROM pairs_per_group
  ),
  kola AS (
    SELECT
      "Id" AS kolo_id,
      "BrojKola",
      "PocetakKola" AS poc,
      "KrajKola" AS kraj,
      ROW_NUMBER() OVER (ORDER BY "BrojKola") AS kolo_seq
    FROM "Kolo"
    WHERE "TakmicenjeId" = v_takmicenje_id
      AND "TipKola" = 1
      AND "Sezona" = v_sezona
    ORDER BY "BrojKola"
  )
  SELECT
    v_base_ut + ROW_NUMBER() OVER (ORDER BY ag.group_round, ag.grp, ag.home_id) AS utakmica_id,
    v_base_st + ROW_NUMBER() OVER (ORDER BY ag.group_round, ag.grp, ag.home_id) AS statistika_id,
    ag.grp,
    kh."Naziv" AS domacin,
    kg."Naziv" AS gost,
    k.kolo_id,
    k."BrojKola",
    ag.group_round,
    (k.poc + random()*(k.kraj-k.poc)) AS datum_ts
  FROM all_games ag
  JOIN "Klub" kh ON kh."Id" = ag.home_id
  JOIN "Klub" kg ON kg."Id" = ag.away_id
  JOIN kola k ON k.kolo_seq = ag.group_round;

  -- Provera
  RAISE NOTICE '=== PROVERA RASPOREDA ===';
  FOR rec IN 
    SELECT 
      "BrojKola",
      COUNT(*) FILTER (WHERE grp = 'A') as grp_a,
      COUNT(*) FILTER (WHERE grp = 'B') as grp_b,
      COUNT(*) FILTER (WHERE grp = 'C') as grp_c,
      COUNT(*) FILTER (WHERE grp = 'D') as grp_d,
      COUNT(*) as total
    FROM tmp_schedule
    GROUP BY "BrojKola"
    ORDER BY "BrojKola"
  LOOP
    RAISE NOTICE 'Kolo %: A=%, B=%, C=%, D=%, Ukupno=%',
      rec."BrojKola", 
      COALESCE(rec.grp_a, 0),
      COALESCE(rec.grp_b, 0),
      COALESCE(rec.grp_c, 0),
      COALESCE(rec.grp_d, 0),
      rec.total;
  END LOOP;

  -- Utakmice
  INSERT INTO "Utakmica"
  ("Id","Uzivo","Domacin","Gost","Lokacija","Rezultat","KoloId","StatistikaId","DatumPocetkaUtakmice")
  SELECT
    s.utakmica_id,
    CASE 
      WHEN s.datum_ts <= v_current_ts 
       AND s.datum_ts + INTERVAL '32 minutes' > v_current_ts 
      THEN TRUE 
      ELSE FALSE 
    END,
    s.domacin,
    s.gost,
    'Bazen ' || s.domacin,
    '0:0',
    s.kolo_id,
    NULL,
    s.datum_ts
  FROM tmp_schedule s;

  -- Statistika
  INSERT INTO "Statistika"
  (
    "Id", "UtakmicaId", "Sport", "TrenutniMinut",
    "GoloviDomacin", "GoloviGost",
    "SutDomacin", "SutGost",
    "SutKaGolDomacin", "SutKaGolGost",
    "VP_PrvaCetDomacin", "VP_DrugaCetDomacin", "VP_TrecaCetDomacin", "VP_CetvCetDomacin",
    "VP_PrvaCetGost", "VP_DrugaCetGost", "VP_TrecaCetGost", "VP_CetvCetGost",
    "IskljucenjaDomacin", "IskljucenjaGost",
    "PeterciDomacin", "PeterciGost",
    "AsistencijeDomacin", "AsistencijeGost",
    "ListaStrelaca"
  )
  SELECT
    s.statistika_id, s.utakmica_id, 3,
    
    CASE
      WHEN s.datum_ts > v_current_ts THEN 0
      WHEN s.datum_ts <= v_current_ts 
       AND s.datum_ts + INTERVAL '32 minutes' > v_current_ts 
      THEN LEAST(EXTRACT(EPOCH FROM (v_current_ts - s.datum_ts))::int / 60, 32)
      ELSE 32
    END,
    
    floor(gd_full * min_factor)::int,
    floor(gg_full * min_factor)::int,
    
    floor(sut_d_full * min_factor)::int,
    floor(sut_g_full * min_factor)::int,
    floor(sut_ka_d_full * min_factor)::int,
    floor(sut_ka_g_full * min_factor)::int,
    
    floor(cet1_d_full * min_factor)::int,
    floor(cet2_d_full * min_factor)::int,
    floor(cet3_d_full * min_factor)::int,
    floor(cet4_d_full * min_factor)::int,
    
    floor(cet1_g_full * min_factor)::int,
    floor(cet2_g_full * min_factor)::int,
    floor(cet3_g_full * min_factor)::int,
    floor(cet4_g_full * min_factor)::int,
    
    floor(iskl_d_full * min_factor)::int,
    floor(iskl_g_full * min_factor)::int,
    
    floor(pet_d_full * min_factor)::int,
    floor(pet_g_full * min_factor)::int,
    
    floor(asist_d_full * min_factor)::int,
    floor(asist_g_full * min_factor)::int,
    
    NULL::text
    
  FROM tmp_schedule s
  CROSS JOIN LATERAL (
    SELECT
      CASE
        WHEN s.datum_ts > v_current_ts THEN 0.0
        WHEN s.datum_ts <= v_current_ts 
         AND s.datum_ts + INTERVAL '32 minutes' > v_current_ts 
        THEN LEAST(EXTRACT(EPOCH FROM (v_current_ts - s.datum_ts)) / (32.0 * 60), 1.0)
        ELSE 1.0
      END AS min_factor
  ) factor
  CROSS JOIN LATERAL (
    SELECT
      (8 + floor(random()*8))::int AS gd_full,
      (6 + floor(random()*7))::int AS gg_full,
      (22 + floor(random()*16))::int AS sut_d_full,
      (22 + floor(random()*16))::int AS sut_g_full,
      (3 + floor(random()*6))::int AS sut_ka_d_full,
      (3 + floor(random()*6))::int AS sut_ka_g_full,
      (2 + floor(random()*7))::int AS iskl_d_full,
      (2 + floor(random()*7))::int AS iskl_g_full,
      floor(random()*3)::int AS pet_d_full,
      floor(random()*3)::int AS pet_g_full,
      (2 + floor(random()*9))::int AS asist_d_full,
      (2 + floor(random()*9))::int AS asist_g_full
  ) stats_full
  CROSS JOIN LATERAL (
    SELECT
      floor(gd_full * 0.25)::int AS cet1_d_full,
      floor(gd_full * 0.25)::int AS cet2_d_full,
      floor(gd_full * 0.20)::int AS cet3_d_full,
      (gd_full - floor(gd_full * 0.25) - floor(gd_full * 0.25) - floor(gd_full * 0.20))::int AS cet4_d_full,
      floor(gg_full * 0.25)::int AS cet1_g_full,
      floor(gg_full * 0.25)::int AS cet2_g_full,
      floor(gg_full * 0.20)::int AS cet3_g_full,
      (gg_full - floor(gg_full * 0.25) - floor(gg_full * 0.25) - floor(gg_full * 0.20))::int AS cet4_g_full
  ) quarters;

  UPDATE "Utakmica" u
  SET "StatistikaId" = s.statistika_id
  FROM tmp_schedule s
  WHERE u."Id" = s.utakmica_id;

  UPDATE "Utakmica" u
  SET "Rezultat" =
    (st."VP_PrvaCetDomacin" + st."VP_DrugaCetDomacin" + 
     st."VP_TrecaCetDomacin" + st."VP_CetvCetDomacin")::text
    || ':' ||
    (st."VP_PrvaCetGost" + st."VP_DrugaCetGost" + 
     st."VP_TrecaCetGost" + st."VP_CetvCetGost")::text
  FROM "Statistika" st
  WHERE u."StatistikaId" = st."Id"
    AND st."Sport" = 3;

  ALTER TABLE "Utakmica" ALTER COLUMN "StatistikaId" SET NOT NULL;

  RAISE NOTICE '';
  RAISE NOTICE '=== STATUS UTAKMICA ===';
  FOR rec IN
    SELECT
      CASE 
        WHEN datum_ts > v_current_ts THEN 'Buduće'
        WHEN datum_ts <= v_current_ts 
         AND datum_ts + INTERVAL '32 minutes' > v_current_ts 
        THEN 'Uživo'
        ELSE 'Završene'
      END AS status,
      COUNT(*) as br
    FROM tmp_schedule
    GROUP BY 
      CASE 
        WHEN datum_ts > v_current_ts THEN 'Buduće'
        WHEN datum_ts <= v_current_ts 
         AND datum_ts + INTERVAL '32 minutes' > v_current_ts 
        THEN 'Uživo'
        ELSE 'Završene'
      END
  LOOP
    RAISE NOTICE '%: % utakmica', rec.status, rec.br;
  END LOOP;

  RAISE NOTICE '';
  RAISE NOTICE '=== ZAVRŠENO ===';
  RAISE NOTICE 'Ukupno: % utakmica', (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM tmp_schedule);

END $$;

COMMIT;
--------------------------------------------------------------------
DODAVANE UTAKMICA STAISTIKOM ZA REGIONALU LGU  VATERPOLU
--------------------------------------------------------------------
BEGIN;

DO $$
DECLARE
  v_takmicenje_id INT := 14;
  v_sezona TEXT := '2025/26';
  v_num_teams INT;
  v_num_rounds INT;
  v_i INT;
  v_j INT;
  v_home_idx INT;
  v_away_idx INT;
  
  -- Nizovi za rotaciju
  v_team_ids INT[];
BEGIN

-- 0) Dozvoli privremeno NULL
ALTER TABLE "Utakmica" ALTER COLUMN "StatistikaId" DROP NOT NULL;

-- 1) Brisanje starih podataka (isto kao u tvojoj skripti)
DELETE FROM "Statistika" s USING "Utakmica" u, "Kolo" k 
WHERE s."UtakmicaId" = u."Id" AND u."KoloId" = k."Id" AND k."TakmicenjeId" = v_takmicenje_id;

DELETE FROM "Utakmica" u USING "Kolo" k 
WHERE u."KoloId" = k."Id" AND k."TakmicenjeId" = v_takmicenje_id;

-- 2) Dohvati sve timove u niz
SELECT array_agg("KlubId" ORDER BY "KlubId") INTO v_team_ids
FROM "Tabela" WHERE "TakmicenjeId" = v_takmicenje_id AND "Sezona" = v_sezona;

v_num_teams := array_length(v_team_ids, 1);

-- Ako je neparan broj timova, dodajemo "fantomski" tim (Bye week logic)
-- Za ovaj primer pretpostavljamo paran broj, ali v_num_rounds je uvek v_num_teams - 1
v_num_rounds := v_num_teams - 1;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS tmp_schedule;
CREATE TEMP TABLE tmp_schedule (
    utakmica_id INT,
    statistika_id INT,
    domacin_id INT,
    gost_id INT,
    kolo_br INT,
    kolo_id INT,
    datum_ts TIMESTAMP
);

-- 3) Generisanje rasporeda rotacionim algoritmom
FOR v_i IN 0..v_num_rounds - 1 LOOP
    FOR v_j IN 0..(v_num_teams / 2) - 1 LOOP
        v_home_idx := (v_i + v_j) % (v_num_teams - 1);
        v_away_idx := (v_num_teams - 1 - v_j + v_i) % (v_num_teams - 1);

        -- Poslednji tim ostaje fiksiran, ostali rotiraju oko njega
        IF v_j = 0 THEN
            v_away_idx := v_num_teams - 1;
        END IF;

        INSERT INTO tmp_schedule (utakmica_id, statistika_id, domacin_id, gost_id, kolo_br)
        VALUES (
            (SELECT COALESCE(MAX("Id"),0) + 1 FROM "Utakmica") + (v_i * (v_num_teams/2) + v_j),
            (SELECT COALESCE(MAX("Id"),0) + 1 FROM "Statistika") + (v_i * (v_num_teams/2) + v_j),
            v_team_ids[v_home_idx + 1],
            v_team_ids[v_away_idx + 1],
            v_i + 1
        );
    END LOOP;
END LOOP;

-- 4) Povezivanje sa tvojom tabelom "Kolo" i dodeljivanje datuma
UPDATE tmp_schedule ts
SET kolo_id = k."Id",
    datum_ts = (k."PocetakKola" + random() * (k."KrajKola" - k."PocetakKola"))
FROM "Kolo" k
WHERE k."TakmicenjeId" = v_takmicenje_id 
  AND k."Sezona" = v_sezona 
  AND k."BrojKola" = ts.kolo_br;

-- 5) Finalni INSERT u Utakmicu
INSERT INTO "Utakmica" ("Id", "Uzivo", "Domacin", "Gost", "Lokacija", "Rezultat", "KoloId", "StatistikaId", "DatumPocetkaUtakmice")
SELECT 
    ts.utakmica_id, 
    (ts.datum_ts::date = CURRENT_DATE),
    kh."Naziv", 
    kg."Naziv",
    'Bazen ' || kh."Naziv",
    '0:0',
    ts.kolo_id,
    NULL,
    ts.datum_ts
FROM tmp_schedule ts
JOIN "Klub" kh ON kh."Id" = ts.domacin_id
JOIN "Klub" kg ON kg."Id" = ts.gost_id;

-- 6) Statistika (tvoj originalni blok, nepromenjen)
INSERT INTO "Statistika" ("Id", "UtakmicaId", "Sport", "TrenutniMinut", "VP_PrvaCetDomacin", "VP_PrvaCetGost", "VP_DrugaCetDomacin", "VP_DrugaCetGost", "VP_TrecaCetDomacin", "VP_TrecaCetGost", "VP_CetvCetDomacin", "VP_CetvCetGost", "AsistencijeDomacin", "AsistencijeGost", "IskljucenjaDomacin", "IskljucenjaGost", "PeterciDomacin", "PeterciGost")
SELECT 
    ts.statistika_id, ts.utakmica_id, 3, 
    CASE WHEN ts.datum_ts::date > CURRENT_DATE THEN 0 WHEN ts.datum_ts::date < CURRENT_DATE THEN 32 ELSE (1 + floor(random()*32))::int END,
    CASE WHEN ts.datum_ts::date > CURRENT_DATE THEN 0 ELSE 1 + floor(random()*5)::int END,
    CASE WHEN ts.datum_ts::date > CURRENT_DATE THEN 0 ELSE 1 + floor(random()*5)::int END,
    CASE WHEN ts.datum_ts::date > CURRENT_DATE THEN 0 ELSE 1 + floor(random()*5)::int END,
    CASE WHEN ts.datum_ts::date > CURRENT_DATE THEN 0 ELSE 1 + floor(random()*5)::int END,
    CASE WHEN ts.datum_ts::date > CURRENT_DATE THEN 0 ELSE 1 + floor(random()*5)::int END,
    CASE WHEN ts.datum_ts::date > CURRENT_DATE THEN 0 ELSE 1 + floor(random()*5)::int END,
    CASE WHEN ts.datum_ts::date > CURRENT_DATE THEN 0 ELSE 1 + floor(random()*5)::int END,
    CASE WHEN ts.datum_ts::date > CURRENT_DATE THEN 0 ELSE 1 + floor(random()*5)::int END,
    CASE WHEN ts.datum_ts::date > CURRENT_DATE THEN 0 ELSE 4 + floor(random()*9)::int END,
    CASE WHEN ts.datum_ts::date > CURRENT_DATE THEN 0 ELSE 4 + floor(random()*9)::int END,
    CASE WHEN ts.datum_ts::date > CURRENT_DATE THEN 0 ELSE floor(random()*5)::int END,
    CASE WHEN ts.datum_ts::date > CURRENT_DATE THEN 0 ELSE floor(random()*5)::int END,
    CASE WHEN ts.datum_ts::date > CURRENT_DATE THEN 0 ELSE floor(random()*3)::int END,
    CASE WHEN ts.datum_ts::date > CURRENT_DATE THEN 0 ELSE floor(random()*3)::int END
FROM tmp_schedule ts;

-- 7) Update StatistikaId i Rezultat
UPDATE "Utakmica" u SET "StatistikaId" = ts.statistika_id FROM tmp_schedule ts WHERE u."Id" = ts.utakmica_id;

UPDATE "Utakmica" u 
SET "Rezultat" = (st."VP_PrvaCetDomacin" + st."VP_DrugaCetDomacin" + st."VP_TrecaCetDomacin" + st."VP_CetvCetDomacin")::text || ':' || (st."VP_PrvaCetGost" + st."VP_DrugaCetGost" + st."VP_TrecaCetGost" + st."VP_CetvCetGost")::text
FROM "Statistika" st WHERE u."StatistikaId" = st."Id" AND st."Sport" = 3;

-- 8) Vrati NOT NULL
ALTER TABLE "Utakmica" ALTER COLUMN "StatistikaId" SET NOT NULL;

RAISE NOTICE 'Raspored generisan uspešno!';
END $$;
COMMIT;
-------------------------------------------------
IZBEGAVANJE NULLABLE VREDONSTI ZA STATISTIKU VATERPOLA
--------------------------------------------------
BEGIN;

DO $$
DECLARE
  v_updated_count INT := 0;
BEGIN

RAISE NOTICE '=== POPULISANJE NULL VREDNOSTI ZA VATERPOLO ===';

-- Update NULL vrednosti u statistikama gde je Sport = 3 (Vaterpolo)
UPDATE "Statistika" st
SET
  -- Četvrtine - ako su NULL, postavi random golove (1-5)
  "VP_PrvaCetDomacin" = COALESCE("VP_PrvaCetDomacin", 1 + floor(random()*5)::int),
  "VP_PrvaCetGost" = COALESCE("VP_PrvaCetGost", 1 + floor(random()*5)::int),
  
  "VP_DrugaCetDomacin" = COALESCE("VP_DrugaCetDomacin", 1 + floor(random()*5)::int),
  "VP_DrugaCetGost" = COALESCE("VP_DrugaCetGost", 1 + floor(random()*5)::int),
  
  "VP_TrecaCetDomacin" = COALESCE("VP_TrecaCetDomacin", 1 + floor(random()*5)::int),
  "VP_TrecaCetGost" = COALESCE("VP_TrecaCetGost", 1 + floor(random()*5)::int),
  
  "VP_CetvCetDomacin" = COALESCE("VP_CetvCetDomacin", 1 + floor(random()*5)::int),
  "VP_CetvCetGost" = COALESCE("VP_CetvCetGost", 1 + floor(random()*5)::int),
  
  -- Asistencije - ako su NULL, postavi 4-12
  "AsistencijeDomacin" = COALESCE("AsistencijeDomacin", 4 + floor(random()*9)::int),
  "AsistencijeGost" = COALESCE("AsistencijeGost", 4 + floor(random()*9)::int),
  
  -- Isključenja - ako su NULL, postavi 0-4
  "IskljucenjaDomacin" = COALESCE("IskljucenjaDomacin", floor(random()*5)::int),
  "IskljucenjaGost" = COALESCE("IskljucenjaGost", floor(random()*5)::int),
  
  -- Peterci (penalty) - ako su NULL, postavi 0-2
  "PeterciDomacin" = COALESCE("PeterciDomacin", floor(random()*3)::int),
  "PeterciGost" = COALESCE("PeterciGost", floor(random()*3)::int)

WHERE st."Sport" = 3
  AND (
    "VP_PrvaCetDomacin" IS NULL OR
    "VP_PrvaCetGost" IS NULL OR
    "VP_DrugaCetDomacin" IS NULL OR
    "VP_DrugaCetGost" IS NULL OR
    "VP_TrecaCetDomacin" IS NULL OR
    "VP_TrecaCetGost" IS NULL OR
    "VP_CetvCetDomacin" IS NULL OR
    "VP_CetvCetGost" IS NULL OR
    "AsistencijeDomacin" IS NULL OR
    "AsistencijeGost" IS NULL OR
    "IskljucenjaDomacin" IS NULL OR
    "IskljucenjaGost" IS NULL OR
    "PeterciDomacin" IS NULL OR
    "PeterciGost" IS NULL
  );

GET DIAGNOSTICS v_updated_count = ROW_COUNT;

RAISE NOTICE 'Ažurirano % statistika sa NULL vrednostima', v_updated_count;

-- Sada updateuj Rezultat u Utakmica tabeli za sve vaterpolo utakmice
UPDATE "Utakmica" u
SET "Rezultat" =
  (st."VP_PrvaCetDomacin" + st."VP_DrugaCetDomacin" + st."VP_TrecaCetDomacin" + st."VP_CetvCetDomacin")::text
  || ':' ||
  (st."VP_PrvaCetGost" + st."VP_DrugaCetGost" + st."VP_TrecaCetGost" + st."VP_CetvCetGost")::text
FROM "Statistika" st
WHERE u."StatistikaId" = st."Id"
  AND st."Sport" = 3
  AND (
    u."Rezultat" = '0:0' OR 
    u."Rezultat" IS NULL OR
    u."Rezultat" !~ '^[0-9]+:[0-9]+$'  -- regex: proveri da li je validan format
  );

GET DIAGNOSTICS v_updated_count = ROW_COUNT;

RAISE NOTICE 'Ažurirano % rezultata u tabeli Utakmica', v_updated_count;

RAISE NOTICE '=== ZAVRŠENO ===';

END $$;

COMMIT;

------------------------------------
DODAVANJE IGRACA TIMOVIMA IZ EVROLIGE
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

DO $$
DECLARE
    v_takmicenje_id INT := 9;
    v_sezona TEXT := '2025/26';

    -- UBACI OVDE ID-jeve klubova (iz Klub.csv)
    klubovi INT[] := ARRAY[149,150,151,152,153,154,155,156,157,158,159,160,161,162];

    klub_id INT;
    i INT;
    igrac_id INT;

    v_games INT;
    v_shots INT;
    v_made  INT;

    v_off INT;
    v_def INT;
    v_reb INT;

    v_age INT;
    v_birthdate DATE;

    v_pos TEXT;
    v_h REAL;
    v_w REAL;
BEGIN
    FOREACH klub_id IN ARRAY klubovi
    LOOP
        FOR i IN 1..12 LOOP

            -- Pozicija + realna visina/tezina po poziciji
            v_pos := CASE
                WHEN i <= 2 THEN 'PG'
                WHEN i <= 4 THEN 'SG'
                WHEN i <= 7 THEN 'SF'
                WHEN i <= 10 THEN 'PF'
                ELSE 'C'
            END;

            v_h := CASE
                WHEN v_pos = 'PG' THEN (180 + random()*12)::REAL   -- 180-192
                WHEN v_pos = 'SG' THEN (185 + random()*13)::REAL   -- 185-198
                WHEN v_pos = 'SF' THEN (193 + random()*12)::REAL   -- 193-205
                WHEN v_pos = 'PF' THEN (198 + random()*12)::REAL   -- 198-210
                ELSE (205 + random()*10)::REAL                     -- 205-215
            END;

            v_w := CASE
                WHEN v_pos = 'PG' THEN (75 + random()*15)::REAL    -- 75-90
                WHEN v_pos = 'SG' THEN (80 + random()*17)::REAL    -- 80-97
                WHEN v_pos = 'SF' THEN (88 + random()*17)::REAL    -- 88-105
                WHEN v_pos = 'PF' THEN (95 + random()*18)::REAL    -- 95-113
                ELSE (105 + random()*18)::REAL                     -- 105-123
            END;

            -- Godine i datum rodjenja
            v_age := (18 + floor(random()*16))::INT;               -- 18..33
            v_birthdate := (CURRENT_DATE - (v_age * 365 + floor(random()*365))::INT);

            -- 1) INSERT IGRAC (tačno tvoje kolone)
            INSERT INTO "Igrac"
            (
                "Ime",
                "Prezime",
                "DatumPocetkaUgovora",
                "DatumKrajaUgovora",
                "Pozicija",
                "Visina",
                "Tezina",
                "DatumRodjenja",
                "ListaKlubova",
                "BrojGodina",
                "KlubID"
            )
            VALUES
            (
                'Igrac_' || klub_id || '_' || i,
                'Prezime_' || i,
                DATE '2025-07-01',
                DATE '2028-06-30',
                v_pos,
                v_h,
                v_w,
                v_birthdate,
                'Klub ' || klub_id,
                v_age,
                klub_id
            )
            RETURNING "Id" INTO igrac_id;

            -- 2) Realne sezonske košarkaške brojke
            v_games := (12 + floor(random()*19))::INT;             -- 12..30 utakmica
            v_shots := (90 + floor(random()*201))::INT;            -- 90..290 suteva
            v_made  := GREATEST(25, (v_shots * (0.35 + random()*0.25))::INT); -- 35%..60%

            v_off := (10 + floor(random()*61))::INT;               -- 10..70
            v_def := (20 + floor(random()*141))::INT;              -- 20..160
            v_reb := v_off + v_def;

            -- 3) INSERT UCINAKIGRACA
            -- Popunjavamo PLAVE kosarkaske kolone + obavezne (Sezona, TakmicenjeId, IgracId)
            -- Ostale (npr. crveni/zuti, distanca, dodavanja...) stavljamo 0 da ne puca ako je NOT NULL.
            INSERT INTO "UcinakIgraca"
            (
                "Pogotci",
                "Asistencije",
                "IndeksKorisnosti",
                "OdigraneUtakmice",
                "IzgubljeneLopte",
                "UkradeneLopte",
                "BlokiraniUdarci",

                "Iskljucenja",
                "Skokovi",
                "SkokoviDF",
                "SkokoviOF",
                "UkupnoFaula",
                "UkupnoSuteva",

                "Sezona",
                "TakmicenjeId",
                "IgracId",

                -- ostale kolone iz tvoje tabele (da budu 0)
                "VraceniPosedi",
                "UkupnoDodavanja",
                "UkupnoTacnihDodavanja",
                "PredjenaDistancaKM",
                "CrveniKartoni",
                "ZutiKartoni"
            )
            VALUES
            (
                v_made,
                (15 + floor(random()*111))::INT,                    -- 15..125
                (90 + floor(random()*261))::INT,                    -- 90..350
                v_games,

                (10 + floor(random()*61))::INT,                     -- 10..70
                (8 + floor(random()*51))::INT,                      -- 8..58
                (5 + floor(random()*46))::INT,                      -- 5..50

                (floor(random()*4))::INT,                           -- 0..3
                v_reb,
                v_def,
                v_off,
                (15 + floor(random()*71))::INT,                     -- 15..85
                v_shots,

                v_sezona,
                v_takmicenje_id,
                igrac_id,

                0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0
            );

        END LOOP;
    END LOOP;
END $$;
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
DODAVANJE IGRACA TIMOVIMA IZ EVRPKUPA
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
DO $$
DECLARE
    v_takmicenje_id INT := 10;
    v_sezona TEXT := '2025/26';

    -- UBACI OVDE ID-jeve klubova (iz Klub.csv)
    klubovi INT[] := ARRAY[163,164,165,166,167,168,169,171,172,173,174,175,176,177,178,179,180,181,182,183,184,185,186,187,188,189,190,191,192,193,194];

    klub_id INT;
    i INT;
    igrac_id INT;

    v_games INT;
    v_shots INT;
    v_made  INT;

    v_off INT;
    v_def INT;
    v_reb INT;

    v_age INT;
    v_birthdate DATE;

    v_pos TEXT;
    v_h REAL;
    v_w REAL;
BEGIN
    FOREACH klub_id IN ARRAY klubovi
    LOOP
        FOR i IN 1..12 LOOP

            -- Pozicija + realna visina/tezina po poziciji
            v_pos := CASE
                WHEN i <= 2 THEN 'PG'
                WHEN i <= 4 THEN 'SG'
                WHEN i <= 7 THEN 'SF'
                WHEN i <= 10 THEN 'PF'
                ELSE 'C'
            END;

            v_h := CASE
                WHEN v_pos = 'PG' THEN (180 + random()*12)::REAL   -- 180-192
                WHEN v_pos = 'SG' THEN (185 + random()*13)::REAL   -- 185-198
                WHEN v_pos = 'SF' THEN (193 + random()*12)::REAL   -- 193-205
                WHEN v_pos = 'PF' THEN (198 + random()*12)::REAL   -- 198-210
                ELSE (205 + random()*10)::REAL                     -- 205-215
            END;

            v_w := CASE
                WHEN v_pos = 'PG' THEN (75 + random()*15)::REAL    -- 75-90
                WHEN v_pos = 'SG' THEN (80 + random()*17)::REAL    -- 80-97
                WHEN v_pos = 'SF' THEN (88 + random()*17)::REAL    -- 88-105
                WHEN v_pos = 'PF' THEN (95 + random()*18)::REAL    -- 95-113
                ELSE (105 + random()*18)::REAL                     -- 105-123
            END;

            -- Godine i datum rodjenja
            v_age := (18 + floor(random()*16))::INT;               -- 18..33
            v_birthdate := (CURRENT_DATE - (v_age * 365 + floor(random()*365))::INT);

            -- 1) INSERT IGRAC (tačno tvoje kolone)
            INSERT INTO "Igrac"
            (
                "Ime",
                "Prezime",
                "DatumPocetkaUgovora",
                "DatumKrajaUgovora",
                "Pozicija",
                "Visina",
                "Tezina",
                "DatumRodjenja",
                "ListaKlubova",
                "BrojGodina",
                "KlubID"
            )
            VALUES
            (
                'Igrac_' || klub_id || '_' || i,
                'Prezime_' || i,
                DATE '2025-07-01',
                DATE '2028-06-30',
                v_pos,
                v_h,
                v_w,
                v_birthdate,
                'Klub ' || klub_id,
                v_age,
                klub_id
            )
            RETURNING "Id" INTO igrac_id;

            -- 2) Realne sezonske košarkaške brojke
            v_games := (12 + floor(random()*19))::INT;             -- 12..30 utakmica
            v_shots := (90 + floor(random()*201))::INT;            -- 90..290 suteva
            v_made  := GREATEST(25, (v_shots * (0.35 + random()*0.25))::INT); -- 35%..60%

            v_off := (10 + floor(random()*61))::INT;               -- 10..70
            v_def := (20 + floor(random()*141))::INT;              -- 20..160
            v_reb := v_off + v_def;

            -- 3) INSERT UCINAKIGRACA
            -- Popunjavamo PLAVE kosarkaske kolone + obavezne (Sezona, TakmicenjeId, IgracId)
            -- Ostale (npr. crveni/zuti, distanca, dodavanja...) stavljamo 0 da ne puca ako je NOT NULL.
            INSERT INTO "UcinakIgraca"
            (
                "Pogotci",
                "Asistencije",
                "IndeksKorisnosti",
                "OdigraneUtakmice",
                "IzgubljeneLopte",
                "UkradeneLopte",
                "BlokiraniUdarci",

                "Iskljucenja",
                "Skokovi",
                "SkokoviDF",
                "SkokoviOF",
                "UkupnoFaula",
                "UkupnoSuteva",

                "Sezona",
                "TakmicenjeId",
                "IgracId",

                -- ostale kolone iz tvoje tabele (da budu 0)
                "VraceniPosedi",
                "UkupnoDodavanja",
                "UkupnoTacnihDodavanja",
                "PredjenaDistancaKM",
                "CrveniKartoni",
                "ZutiKartoni"
            )
            VALUES
            (
                v_made,
                (15 + floor(random()*111))::INT,                    -- 15..125
                (90 + floor(random()*261))::INT,                    -- 90..350
                v_games,

                (10 + floor(random()*61))::INT,                     -- 10..70
                (8 + floor(random()*51))::INT,                      -- 8..58
                (5 + floor(random()*46))::INT,                      -- 5..50

                (floor(random()*4))::INT,                           -- 0..3
                v_reb,
                v_def,
                v_off,
                (15 + floor(random()*71))::INT,                     -- 15..85
                v_shots,

                v_sezona,
                v_takmicenje_id,
                igrac_id,

                0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0
            );

        END LOOP;
    END LOOP;
END $$

    klubovi INT[] := ARRAY[198,199,207,208,210,213,217,219,220,221,222,224,225,196,200,201,202,203,204,205,206,209,211,212,215,216,218,223,197];
